Here are the requirements:
1. Strictly output a JSON.
2. The instructions must be in English.
3. Use diverse verbs in your responses to generalize better. This is very important!
4. A small language model should be able to complete the instruction. For example, do not ask the assistant to create any visual or audio output. For another example, do not ask the assistant to wake you up at 5pm or set a reminder because it cannot perform any action.
